| <span data-ttu-id="4ef85-452">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef85-452">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4ef85-453">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef85-453">Value</span></span> |
